CR 24 -6 Recommending FIRST READING of Bill 126, CD1 (2023), to repeal 
Chapter 19.62 - Flood Hazard Areas, establish Chapter 16.29 - Flood Hazard 
Areas, transfer the responsibility for administering Flood Hazard Areas from the 
Director of Planning to the Director of Public Works, and include the Federal 
Emergency Management Agency’s requirement that all machinery and 
equipment servicing a building be elevated to one foot above the base -flood 
elevation.

Council of the County of Maui  on 2024-01-12 9:00 AM - Regular Meeting
2024. The council of the county of maui regular meeting for JANUARY 12th, 2024. Q. [Gavel] . Will the council 
meeting of JANUARY 12th, 2024 please come to order. MADAM Clerk, roll call. >> chair, proceeding with roll call, 
council member pro tempore tasha kama. >> o her way. >> vice-chair ek le sugimura. >> good morning everyone, so 
wonderful to have the chimbers filled with all these wonderful people, looking forward to a great meeting. Thank you, 
chair.\r\n\r\n>> council member tamara paltin. >> aloha kakahiaka. >> council member gabe johnson. >> aloha, chair, 
council members, community members I'm here and ready to work. >> chair, we'll skip member rawlins-fernandez,
